<header class="entry-header">
<h1 class="entry-title">Drop-In Tutoring</h1>
</header><!-- .entry-header -->


<div class="entry-content">

<blockquote>
<p style="text-align: center"><b>Welcome to the Spring 2026 semester!</b><br />
Tutoring will be available between Monday, February 9th, and Tuesday, May 12, 2026.<br />
Wishing you a successful semester, and we look forward to seeing you!</p>
<p style="text-align: center"><a class="button button-primary" href="http://traccloud.go-redrock.com/umbc/">Undergraduate Students &#8211; Schedule ASC Services Here</a></p>
</blockquote>
<div style="text-align: center"></div>
<p>Drop-in tutoring (located in the Library) is recommended for students who have quick questions. Students who would like more in-depth assistance should make a <a href="https://academicsuccess.umbc.edu/appointment-tutoring/">tutoring appointment</a>.</p>
<p>Peer support for specific courses depends on resources available each semester. Looking for a different course? Please visit our <a href="https://academicsuccess.umbc.edu/tutoring/"><strong>main tutoring page</strong></a> to view other support options.</p>
<p><span class="first-child" data-contrast="auto">If you have any questions about drop-in tutoring, please email </span><a class="last-child first-child" href="mailto:tutoring@umbc.edu"><span class="first-child last-child" data-contrast="none">tutoring@umbc.edu</span></a>.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2>Available Courses</h2>
<ul class="list-inline" aria-label="Available courses navigation">
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#Biol101">Biology</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#Chem101">Chemistry</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#cmpe212">Computer Engineering</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#cmsc201">Computer Science</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#Econ101">Economics</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#ges102">Geographical and Environmental Systems</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#is147">Information Systems</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#Math104">Math</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#Phys111">Physics</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#sci100">Science</a></li>
<li><a class="button button-primary" href="#span101">Spanish</a></li>

</ul>

<h3>Computer Science Courses</h3>
<p>Tutors also <b>provide support with programming languages for all students, regardless of major or course</b>. The tutoring provided by the ASC for computing courses is offered in partnership with the <a href="https://coeit.umbc.edu/">College of Engineering and Information Technology</a> and is supplemental to the support provided by the <a href="https://coeit.umbc.edu/csee-dept/">Department of Computer Science and Electrical Engineering</a>, the <a href="https://coeit.umbc.edu/is-dept/">Department of Information Systems</a> Graduate Teaching Assistants and the Undergraduate Teaching Fellows assigned to the respective courses.</p>
